meter_icon( id : string ) {
      const type = this.meter(id).type
      if ( type === 'KV' ) return this.Meter_icon_water_cold()
      if ( type === 'SV' ) return this.Meter_icon_water_hot()
      return this.Meter_icon_energy()
}

  body = undefined as string | Buffer | NodeJS.ReadableStream | undefined

  constructor(props: AcmeServerResponseProps & { body?: string | Buffer | NodeJS.ReadableStream | Object | undefined }) {
    Object.assign(this, props)
    const body = props.body

    if (body && typeof body === 'object') {
      const isStream = typeof (body as { on?: Function }).on === 'function'

      if (!(props.body instanceof Buffer) && !isStream) {
        if (!props.contentType) this.contentType = 'application/json'
        this.body = JSON.stringify(props.body)
      }
    }
  }

–≤–æ—Ç, —è –Ω–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞–ª –¥–ª—è —Å–µ–±—è —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –ø–∞—Ä—Å–µ—Ä/—Å–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –≤–µ–±—Å–æ–∫–µ—Ç–æ–≤ –≤ 60 —Å—Ç—Ä–æ—á–µ–∫
let Clients = new Set();
require(`tls`).createServer({ cert: fs.readFileSync(`${__dirname}/../ssl-cert/server.cert`), key: fs.readFileSync(`${__dirname}/../ssl-cert/server.key`) }, socket => {
  socket.setKeepAlive(false);
  socket.setNoDelay(true);
  socket.on(`error`, (err) => console.log(`--socket error:`, err));
  socket.once(`data`, async (chunk) => {
    let str = chunk.toString();
    let wsInKeyIndex = str.indexOf(`Sec-WebSocket-Key: `) + `Sec-WebSocket-Key: `.length;
    let wsInKey = str.slice(wsInKeyIndex, str.indexOf(`\r\n`, wsInKeyIndex));
    let wsOutKey = require(`crypto`).createHash(`sha1`).update(`${wsInKey}258EAFA5-E914-47DA-95CA-C5AB0DC85B11`, `binary`).digest(`base64`);
    socket.write(`HTTP/1.1 101 Switching Protocols\r\nUpgrade: websocket\r\nConnection: Upgrade\r\nSec-WebSocket-Accept: ${wsOutKey}\r\n\r\n`);
    let [buf, tempBuf, waitPromise] = [Buffer.alloc(0), Buffer.alloc(0), null];
    let processChunk = () => {
      if (waitPromise !== null && buf.length >= waitPromise.bytes) {
        [tempBuf, buf] = [buf.slice(0, waitPromise.bytes), buf.slice(waitPromise.bytes)];
        waitPromise.resolve(tempBuf);
        waitPromise = null;
      }
    };
    let readBytes = (n) => buf.length >= n ? ([tempBuf, buf] = [buf.slice(0, n), buf.slice(n)], tempBuf) : new Promise(res => waitPromise = { bytes: n, resolve: res });
    socket.on(`data`, chunk => (buf = Buffer.concat([buf, chunk]), processChunk()));
    socket.on(`close`, () => (console.log(`--ws: socket closed`), Clients.delete(send)));
    let send = (output) => {
      try {
        let data = Buffer.from(output);
        let wsMessage = Buffer.concat([Buffer.alloc(2 + (data.length < 126 ? 0 : data.length < 65536 ? 2 : 8)), data]);
        wsMessage[0] = 0b10000001;
        wsMessage[1] = data.length < 126 ? data.length : data.length < 65536 ? (wsMessage.writeUInt16BE(data.length, 2), 126) : (wsMessage.writeBigUInt64BE(BigInt(data.length), 2), 127)
        socket.write(wsMessage);
      } catch (err) {
        socket.destroy(err);
      }
    }
    Clients.add(send);
    try {
      while (true) {
        let twoBytes = await readBytes(2);
        if (twoBytes[0] !== 0b10000001 && twoBytes[0] !== 0b10001000) throw Error(`--ws: non-text opcode and non-fin: ${twoBytes[0].toString(2)}`);
        let length = (twoBytes[1] & 0b01111111) < 126 ? twoBytes[1] & 0b01111111 : (twoBytes[1] & 0b01111111) === 126 ? (await readBytes(2)).readUInt16BE(0) : Number((await readBytes(8)).readBigUInt64BE(0));
        let mask = (twoBytes[1] & 0b10000000) !== 0 ? await readBytes(4) : null;
        let data = await readBytes(length);
        if (mask !== null) for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i += 1) data[i] ^= mask[i & 3];
        if (data.length === 0) { console.log(`--ws: zero length data, opcode:${twoBytes[0].toString(2)}`); continue; }
        if (twoBytes[0] === 0b10001000) { console.log(`--ws: connection closed`, data.readUint16BE(0)); continue; }
        try {
          let input = JSON.parse(data.toString());
          let result = process(input);
          send(JSON.stringify(result));
        } catch (err) {
          console.log(err);
          console.log(`--opcode: ${twoBytes[0].toString(2)}`);
          console.log(data);
          console.log(data.toString());
        }
      };
    } catch (err) {
      socket.destroy(err);
    }
  });
}).listen({ host: `0.0.0.0`, port: 3001 }, () => console.log(`--wss listen`));
